Compilation Committee of Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Words

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon Jo

1)
The Main Current of Providence
Here in the West, we write horizontally, but in the East, we write vertically. Now, the horizontal and vertical must come together. Why do we write to the left instead of to the right? Have you thought about that? "Because we are trying to go from Satan's side to God's side." (Laughter) You can think of it that way. Ultimately, what it means is that it goes from a dark place to a bright place; I see that the principle of creation is like that. 
How is the Will of Providence Fulfilled?
Furthermore, the light is given by God who is above, shining down into the darkness. Therefore, Western civilization must turn to the East, and Eastern civilization must turn to the West. The East is where the sun rises. It rises and then goes this way. After that, it goes over there and turns back in the opposite direction. It goes from the East to the West. After returning, it must come down and then go up again. What does that mean? If God is light and ideals, then light, ideals, and everything must come to humanity, and humanity must return it to God. Everything returning is the principle of it.
Do you know why Western people's eyes are so big? It's because they look at things up close. It's realism, it's pragmatism. The civilization created by people with big eyes becomes a realistic civilization. Isn't that right? "That's right." People with small eyes look far away. Isn't that so? When you look far away, your eyes narrow. They don't get bigger. So, Reverend Moon's eyes are small. That's a characteristic. (Laughter) It's not a laughing matter. I don't have time to talk about that today, but think about it. That's the truth. Because of that, people with big eyes are afraid of the present, while those with small eyes are not afraid. It's relative. (Laughter)
Now, then, the current of providence... You will know when you encounter the current. Who is the one who seizes providence and pushes it forward? "God." It is God! Then, who is the one who forms the current of providence? "Humans." That's right, it is humans.
However, we humans, like water, cannot create water. Water exists naturally. Water is something that is originally there. So how does water come into being? It comes down as rain from above, and it also rises from below. Isn't that right? It combines to form a current of water. In that sense, God's will of providence is something that God has prepared, but it cannot happen with God alone; the upper and lower must come together.
Humans Must Follow the Current of Providence
Now, we know that rain comes and goes. Then, does a small stream of water become a big river like the Hudson River? What do you think? If you look at the Hudson River, do you think there is more rainwater or spring water? "There is more rainwater." How much percentage do you think? (Laughter) It will probably be over 90 percent. And the bigger the river, is its current shorter or longer? "Longer." The longer it is, the bigger the river will be.
Then, can the source where the river starts be completely different? There are many types of rivers, small and large, but can the shape of where the river starts be different? Is it the same or different? "It's the same." It's the same. When you think about everything, the source is the same. What is the difference? The difference is where it stops. If the environment is not prepared, it will naturally stop. You must understand this. You must know that the environment is an absolute requirement.
Now, there is a drop of dew hanging on a leaf. This drop of dew says, "I may be small, but I will move with all the water of the world! Wherever I go, all the water will follow!" That statement is correct. When this drop of dew falls into the current of the Hudson River, that statement is true. The whole world is following it. Isn't that right? Is that right or not? "That's right." However, if that drop of dew falls on a rock or on the ground when the wind blows, what will happen? (Laughter) In that case, what is the bragging about? It all becomes a lie. So one is correct, and one is fundamentally wrong. Is that right or not? "That's right."
In the same way, the principle applies to fulfilling the will of providence. So if there is a long current flowing, if you can "plop" into that flow, the bigger the river, the more magnificent it is. Do you think so too? "Yes." So if you look at the flow of thought in our human world, it is the same. The flow of thought is the same, and the flow of providence is the same.
Now, when we look at religion today, until now, humanity has been trying to find religions with a long history. What is different about our Christianity is that the current of thought centered on the Christian Bible today started from the first ancestors of humanity. Adam and Eve went down through the current of God's providence and fell from there.
Then, what would be like that river current? What is it? It is the current of love. The current of providence is the current of love. So, is love different? Is love different now than it was in the past? "No." Is it the same? "Yes." What is it? In America, they are making a fuss about same-sex marriage now. "No." (Laughter) It is the same, it is the same.
So, if this fell into the current of love, how much... But where did it fall? Where? In a place like a desert. (Laughter) So, what is the world like now? When viewed from the center of love, it is a desert-like world, a world like a rock. This has become a world where everything does not connect. So, this water that fell on the rock is evaporating and floating around. It is the same with you all. Now, you have become like a drop of water, floating around like this, wherever you go.
So, they are trying to create a cloud centered around clubs that resonate with each other. So, the place where the vapor stays is a high mountain. If there is a high mountain, it starts to gather here (while drawing). Where does it start to combine? Generally, it is difficult to combine, but it combines when it hits the mountain. So, the statement that religious movements or idealistic movements start in the mountains is valid. That's right. It is all the same. Buddhism is centered around mountains, Christianity is centered around mountains, Moses too... it is all about mountains.
Religion Seeks a High and Harmonious Spiritual Ideal
What is interesting? When you go to such mountains, the term "living water" does not refer to water that comes from flatlands. Isn't that interesting? Is that so? "Yes." It is a fact that spring water must come from high mountains. Does spring water come from high mountains? "Yes." Therefore, the clean water that can combine is the water that comes from the earth and the vapor. That is correct. Isn't it? The spring water that comes from the mountain and the vapor... Rain comes well from high mountains. When you see that, you can assure that many movements have occurred centered around the mountains.
Globally, where is the highest mountain? "Mount Everest." When you go to a place like Mount Everest, you feel a new taste, a fresh taste. So, what occupies the high mountain? "Snow." What is that snow? "Water." It is water that has gathered.
When you look at it this way, what does it symbolize? White symbolizes victory, authority, and strength. Is that right? "Yes." The higher the mountain, the more magnificent it is, but when you see it, you say, "It is high," but if there is only snow, you say, "Ah." If there is snow at the top, you say, "Ah." Isn't that so? "Yes." When you see that, water is the source of life. Isn't that so?
All living beings are made up of 75% water. Where there is harmony in water, there is life. When you have more water, you feel refreshed, right? When there is less water, you supply water, right? You know that controlling your body temperature at 36.7 degrees or so is all about water. It controls all life. Isn't that so? When you see that, water is absolutely necessary. From that perspective, what are you now? "Vapor." You are vapor, vapor. Vapor is all wandering.
Now, where does it collide? (While drawing) What is it? Religion is like making mountains in the human world. It is pursuing a spiritual mountain... Therefore, it is seeking a spiritual ideal. Do you prefer flatlands or mountains? "Mountains are better." White people all like flatlands, right? "No." Texas, Arizona, they are all flat. Isn't that so in America? What about the Indians? "They like mountains." (Laughter) There are two types. In the East, if you look, it is all mountainous areas centered around Mount Everest. Therefore, a harmonious terrain is good for taste and everything else.
From that perspective, a country like Korea is truly beautiful. I am not saying this just because I am Korean. It is all true. Why? Because when I drive in America, I can fall asleep in less than five minutes. But in Korea, you can't sleep even if you want to. Every alley is full of changes. (Laughter) But I am not saying everyone should come to Korea. Even if you come, there are worries. (Laughter) When you see it this way, you realize that harmony is necessary.
The Unification Church is Like a High Mountain with a Continuous Flow of Living Water
Now, we have a mountain called the Unification Church. Is the Unification Church a big mountain or a small mountain? "It is a big mountain." Is it a flat mountain like Mount Fuji, or is it a mountain like this? (While drawing) "It is a mountain with changes." How much change is there? Even while sleeping, it is good, even while going to the bathroom, it is good... (Laughter) The Unification Church members are complicated. 
Then, the wandering vapor can catch on anywhere. The greater the difference, the better. Going back and forth, the area of collision is large, and there are many places to catch, so is there less rain? More? "More." Is this a sand mountain or a rock mountain? "A rock mountain." Would a sand mountain be like this? A rock mountain must be like this; a sand mountain cannot be like this at all. So, do you like rock mountains or sand mountains? "We like rock mountains." If you are not careful, it can be dangerous. You can slip and fall, but on a sand mountain, you can slide anywhere, and it is safe. It is all good. You can sleep well, and you can roll around safely. However, here, you must hold on to something wherever you go. You must wear a belt to sleep. (Laughter) That is how it is.
But earlier, I said there is a spring on this mountain. If it is a spring from Mount Fuji, what is the spring water that comes from the top of a sand mountain? Is that spring water clean or dirty? "Good." What is good? What this means is that it is all mixed with sand. It looks murky. If there is living water on this mountain (rock mountain), what would it be like? "Very clean." (Laughter) However, would it be easy or difficult to find that living water? Would there be many spring currents coming out? "Few."
If there is living water here... If living water is here, everyone would say, "Ah, I drank living water from Mount Fuji." If there is someone bragging about drinking living water from a high mountain, and someone else who drank living water from Mount Fuji or another mountain, who would be bragging? "From the rock." Everyone knows that. (Laughter)
Then, what is good water? It is 100% necessary for the human body. Now, as soon as you enter here, even if you sweat it all out, you must know that the sweat itself is clean. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Then, if you sleep there, how delicious will your sleep be, and how good will it feel to breathe, and how light will your body feel? Just think about it. Then what will happen? You won't be able to stay still. "Hey, I feel so good, I want to jump with all my might. Even when I sing, I want to be the best, and in everything, I want to be the best." Isn't that right? You want to shout louder than anyone in history, you want to make the whole world resonate with your voice. Isn't that so? "Yes."
Is our Unification Church a high mountain or a low mountain? "It is a high mountain." A high mountain, that is good. Then, are you all vapor that becomes and disappears? "No." What kind of people are you? So what will happen? Are you all combining? You say, "Hey, you came from the West..." (The recording briefly cuts out) What will happen then? You become one, one. When you become one and continue like this, due to the temperature difference, when the vapor gathers in this mountain where the wind is strong and cold, it will rain immediately. It will rain right there. The water that falls as rain is also clean water. 
God Wants Strong, Tenacious, and Resilient People
Then, should it flow and then stop, or should it continue? "It should continue." Then what should happen? Here, a big spring must burst forth like a fountain and flow. (While drawing) Now, if there is a continuous flow of water that does not stop through spring, summer, autumn, and winter, then the next issue arises. Here, if it is complicated, and there are many spring currents, the droplets that fall can happen even daily. It goes out like this. It keeps getting bigger.
Everyone, where is the highest place in America? "Right here." (Laughter)
(clapping) Look at this. It's not Whitney Mountain. The highest and most dangerous place is Belvedere or Barrytown. You need to know that. Right? Isn’t that so? "If you go, it’s dangerous. Don’t go. Anyone, whether a man or a woman, will be in big trouble." It’s a big fuss. Right? "That’s right." So what about you all? Where are the people who are here? They are climbing up right now. This mountain, you know, if it just stood still, it wouldn’t be known, but if this mountain shook like rubber when the wind blew, wouldn’t that be great? (laughter) Then everyone would fall. Wouldn’t they? So, if we put shackles on this mountain, do you think it would be like a cage with the door locked? You need to think about that too. Why? Because God wants to pick the best, the number one in the world, in any sport or anything throughout history. He is trying to pick one person. To do that, if the mountain is still, anyone can climb it, but even if the mountain is upside down, you have to hold on and stay there. That’s what I mean. That’s why black people come here, white people come here, and Asians come here. Everyone has this heart that says, "I will reach the top." If you don’t have that heart, then… So, in the end, who do you think will remain? The son of a rich family or the son of a poor family? "The son of a poor family." Then what should you do? Be tough and resilient like this…

If there’s a tree on this mountain, and it grows, how wonderful would that be? God enjoys looking at that mountain, but in the end, what happens? If there’s a green tree here, He will look at that one and say, "Wow!" And if all the trees die and only this one remains green and stretches out, how much will we praise it? That’s wonderful. If there’s someone taking pictures, would they take this or that? Which one would they take? You all would feel the same way, wouldn’t you? Wouldn’t you? "Yes." 

So you came to the Unification Church, and the teacher will look for someone who, despite suffering, does not shrink back but stands tall and stretches out like a fresh branch. If there’s living water under this stream, how great would that be? Then the trees living in such a place would be trees that have everything in the world, a tree worthy of boasting throughout history. If such a tree could grow infinitely, how big would it be? Think about it. No matter how strong the wind blows… it would penetrate through the rocks. How about you? Wouldn’t that be great? "Yes." 

Then, if through the spring water it goes into the roots of the pine tree and becomes a single drop of water falling from the tip of the leaves, how proud would that be? If you look through history, there’s probably nothing more welcomed than this in the history of water. Our Unification Church is the same. God is doing such a history. Look. Reverend Moon, where would he be in terms of this mountain? If there’s this mountain, at first, there’s nothing, right? In the midst of having no life, the stream bursts forth, and spring water begins to flow. If God is there, He would want that the most.

How hard would it be to break through the rock? If there’s gold here, it would want to break through. It would get blocked here, and then it would get blocked again, and again… (drawing while speaking) There would be all sorts of circumstances, wouldn’t there? Water flows down through the holes made here. When you think about that, you would want to be connected here, saying, "Oh, what is this?" Then when you come out from the top, you would say, "Oh, what is that? Oh, I want to go there." And you would connect again, and here too… That’s how it’s meant to be, isn’t it? God would think that way too. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." So Reverend Moon thinks it would be good to make such holes. When God sees that, He wants it too, saying, "Hey, good job. Keep going! Yes! Yes!" and supports it.

Then when it explodes and bursts out, how would it be? (laughs) So when the water stream spreads from the top and disperses into vapor, if a rainbow spreads out like that, everyone would say, "Ah! Look at that!" Then here, Americans, those who want to be number one in the world, would go first by helicopter and say, "It’s mine." (laughs) That’s how it would be. It can happen. So if the spring water bursts forth, what kind of problem would that create? It would be amazing. If people want to see the scenery, they would all have to come here, drink the water once, and not only drink it but also want to feel good, look at the whole world, think about it, and dream about it. Wouldn’t they want to feel good and sleep beside it? Would they want to go down from there or live there? "They would want to live." That’s how it would be.

What is most important to God? Think about what is most important to God. God doesn’t need money. Does He need power? "No." Does He need knowledge? "No." What does He need? What could God possibly need? "Love." Why does He need love? Why is love good? Why does God need love? Look. The reason it’s good is that in good places, everything is completely good. The eyes that like it are the best, the nose that likes it is the best, hearing is the best, eating is the best, touching is the best, and thinking is the best. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." It’s one hundred percent good.

You need to rise above the standard of fallen love. So, our young men and women, when you reach puberty, speaking of you young women, in the West, when you turn fourteen, it’s usually like this, right? Breasts grow, hips grow, and all this strange climate arises within you, and you feel all fidgety, and your eyes become three-dimensional, your ears become three-dimensional, and it all becomes strange. (laughs) At that time, even if you try to keep your mouth shut, you end up doing this. (making expressions, laughter) Strange signs arise. When you see autumn leaves rolling, you laugh and say, "Ho ho ho." (laughs) Everything is strange.

What is that? Why does that happen? Even those who were quiet start to wander around. They want to float in the air. Have you all felt that? "Yes." (laughs) At that time, everyone is like a poet, everyone is like a literary person. When there’s a sign of love or something centered around oneself, everything becomes concentrated. So first love… You need to understand that for fallen humans, first love is within the standard of the fallen realm. Do you understand? So you need to start from a place of love that is higher than first love. You need to rise. Isn’t that right? "That’s right."

On the path to find heaven, if you cannot find a love that is higher than the first love of the world, centered around heaven, there is no way to return to heaven. Then, to achieve that, what should you do? Centering on the partner of your first love, you dedicate your life, then it becomes a matter of life, then a matter of material, then a matter of knowledge, and then a matter of power; everything becomes a problem. (drawing while speaking) If two people who are desperately in love want to enter the will of heaven, they must find a love that can let go of these things within a week. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

This level, you need to rise to a level higher than this, and only then can you connect and explode. Boom! It explodes. It’s like lightning striking from the sky. A lightning of love occurs. When that happens, everyone reconciles and becomes one. No matter how much you throw it away or put it in a sizzling fire, love does not change. Do you understand? "Yes."

Then the eyes become the best eyes, the ears become the best ears, the nose becomes the best nose, the mouth becomes the best mouth, and the heart becomes the best heart… (laughs) You all, try to keep your mouth shut and hold your nose tightly. When you reach the brink of death, saying "I’m going to die!" try to breathe out. (gesturing) It’s better than that. It’s a level better than that. Do you understand what I mean?

That’s why even when you’re about to die, you end up thinking about your partner; you can’t think of anything else. Do you understand? You all feel the same way, right? "Yes." At that time, you white people would think, "Oh, their face is so pale. Oh, their face is so yellow. Their face is so black." Wouldn’t you? "No." Black and white would reconcile at once with an "Ah." You need to enter a realm without thought, a realm of that kind.

So why is God good? Because God is the subject of love. When He breathes the breath of love, it needs to be in sync, "Hoo—hoo—, hoo—hoo—, hoo—hoo—" (breathing in and out) That’s possible because of that. Isn’t it? The distance between God and man must always be the same; if it’s even a little smaller, it keeps getting smaller. In the end, it stops. It’s bound to stop. Similarly, if you just break through once, God would truly say, "Ah! That’s good!" and people would say, "Ah! That’s good! That’s good! That’s good!" (laughs) This is what you should try to make last for a thousand years. If you become one, the closer you get, the better it is…

So, when I talk about this… When a man hugs a woman, it feels like the waist disappears, and you feel that "eventually, there’s no waist." It feels like it’s gone. So, you have to reach a level where you say "It’s gone," and only then does "It is" begin. You have to say "It’s gone" to say "It is," and you have to say "It is" to say "It’s gone."

So, why does God like love? If God has five senses, all the sensations of the five senses become one, and God enjoys it, opening His mouth and laughing, "Ha! Ha!" and the universe plays along. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." So, I talked about this at the recent scientists' conference, but the human body is double. This (drawing) is like a single sound box. If you strike this, even if this one doesn’t get hit, it’s the same… Do you understand? Then this spreads out. So, when these two resonate, what kind of phenomenon occurs? It creates a three-dimensional effect. If there’s a person like this, it becomes a big sound box, and if there’s a sound box centered around God, it resonates, "Bing—" When this happens, it goes "Boom—." Here, if the men strike "Bang!" and these two become one, it goes "Ding!" and the woman goes "Ding!" When the two become one, then God resonates. (laughs) It has to be like that…

So, why do men need women, and why do women need men? To resonate with God’s love. Then what happens? "Ah! That’s good!" You feel good even if you don’t eat or sleep. So, do you women need men? "Yes." You men, do you need women? "Yes." Why, why? Only when the love of a perfect man and woman resonates can God’s love be complete… That’s why religion must be a place where the power of love that transcends the love of worldly men and women is involved. (recording momentarily cuts out)

American women also want to absolutely believe in and follow Reverend Moon, and you all, American youth also want to absolutely believe in and follow Reverend Moon. There’s that strange power. Young men and women are willing to risk their lives for the path of first love, but once they taste the essence of the Unification Church, it’s not just about life; they would go even if it means death.

And if you don’t listen well to the teacher’s words or don’t act on what is said, pain comes, and if you follow the teacher’s words, even if it’s hard, you feel strength. Isn’t that so? "That’s right." That kind of action occurs. In fact, if I directly guide you, it would be faster. If I guide each individual’s heart, everything gets entangled. The teacher is in your hearts, right? "Yes."

Why is that? Today, in this world of life, the sun is central. Wherever the sun goes, it can go anywhere. God’s love is the eternal sun of life. Do you understand what I mean? You are undergoing such training right now. That’s why when you go to the spirit world, everything adjusts according to the direction centered around God.

So right now, you are in the position of a drop of water, and you need to become a resonant body like this. Pure, pure water! It must be water that true people of the world can drink and also pure water that God can drink. Your hearts are pure, but how about your bodies? They are dirty. But your hearts have also been dirtied. So when you think of "God’s love," you need to feel that it resonates from your hearts, "Woo—" Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

So what does God need? "Love." Why does He need love? "So that He can be happy when He sees it…" That’s right. Only then can God truly rejoice. The absolute God rejoices absolutely.

So, if I hit you, should this change? No matter how much I hit you, should it change or not? "It should not change." Like pure gold, the more you go into the crucible, the more you should shine. When you go into the crucible, will there be a lot of things to burn or few? "Few." There should be nothing to burn. If you put you into the crucible, will there be black smoke or white smoke? "White smoke." (laughs) Let’s stop with the smoke; there will be steam.

Look. Reverend Moon is a person who came out of Korea. Flowing like a river from the foundation that God has prepared, it passes through Korea, then Japan, crosses the Pacific, comes into America, and then goes through Europe… Now it is flowing like a stream. So, just like those living by the Hudson River drink the water of the Hudson, in the future, there is a possibility that everything will move under the influence of the Unification Church. Is it delicious water or tasteless water? "Delicious water." How much? Fresh and pleasant, good for the eyes, good for the ears, and all five senses are good!
That's why people who join the Unification Church cannot live anywhere else. When I went to Korea this time, I heard that someone who had left the Unification Church was crying, saying, "Oh, I want to see the teacher, but I can't go." Do you understand what that means? 
"Yes." Is the Unification Church a good place, is it fresh water? "Yes." Now, with this, it is currently influential worldwide... In America, when you say "Moonie," it has become a term. These days, it even appears in cartoons and has become an interesting anecdote. At first, I thought I would just taste it, but on the day I just tasted it, I became so alert that I thought, "Wow!" and that was an accident. I wish that wasn't the case, but because it is, the America that opposed it is in big trouble. This is because, with America's military power and political power, no matter how much they try to provide top-notch education to the citizens, it won't work. (Cheers. Applause) 
Our Unification Church members, you know, have suffered after joining, but when you look at their faces, they shine. When we went to Korea this time, it became known that "people who join the Unification Church do not age." They thought that once you join the Unification Church, everyone would become ugly and miserable, but instead, everyone became vibrant. They said, "Oh, even though they are that old, they look young." Do you understand what that means? 
Look. How much worry is there in the world right now? "Oh, what will happen if I go out like this?" they wonder. How dangerous it is... Think about it. Is there any day that is comfortable? Think about it. So, you Unification Church members... Clean water is always blue. Is that true? Is it blue? "Yes." In summer, the leaves are green, right? It becomes green because it absorbs a lot of blue water. Since it absorbs all the blue water, it looks green. Have you thought about that? "Yes." 
So you are blue, always? "Yes." When you see blue eyes, you know, if you look into them, they are attractive, and similarly, the more you see Unification Church members, the more attractive they become? Everyone is interested in our Unification Church, and when they see us, they say, "Wow! The Moonies are here, the Moonies are here," and both high and low people, especially young people, are just curious about "Where are the Moonies going?" Right? Isn't that so? "That's right." When the kings, princes, and princesses of the heavenly kingdom appear, the world is like that. People's hearts are like that. But when you look closely, it's not a bad thing; it's a wonderful thing. "Wow!" and at first, they are like this with their ears... (Gestures. Laughter) 
Moonies revolutionize history based on love and sweep the world. 
We are different. The flow is different. It flows in all directions, east, west, south, and north. But ordinary people only flow to the east; we are going around all directions. So if you study about Moonies, you won't be able to understand this. When they are fundraising and they are so hungry that they can't eat and are about to die, when evening comes and they come in like this, their mother comes and says, "I will definitely treat you well, let's go, oh, you have worked hard! I love you, let's go, let's go," but they still refuse. (Laughter) You can't understand that. (Applause) 
You all have eyes here and behind you, and eyes in all directions, but they do not know that. Right? "That's right." So it connects everywhere. Clean water flows everywhere. So, because of that, just listen to my words for three days and live like that. What will happen? Is it good or bad? If you feed them words and give them water, everything that was blocked until now will be cleared, and they will feel refreshed, saying, "Oh, so this is who God is. So this is how the world is." 2)
Reevaluation of Existing Values and Exploration of Absolute Values
Respected chairperson, and distinguished professors and scholars from around the world! I sincerely welcome all of you who are attending the 7th International Conference on Scientific Unification today. I hope that this conference, where the wisdom of the world gathers to discuss the theme of "Reevaluation of Existing Values and Exploration of Absolute Values," will become a source of eternal truth and hope that illuminates future history. 
Absolute values can only be found within the ideals of the universe's first cause
Modern civilization has produced a directionless nihilism as a byproduct, and the masses have become intoxicated with machines and momentary hedonism. As a result, humanity is ruthlessly standardizing and objectifying individuality, forgetting human dignity and each person's nature. Truly, today, this world is a world of chaos and disorder. This chaos and disorder are not limited to any specific individual or society; they are serious issues that span individuals, families, societies, nations, and the entire world. 
Some analyze the problems of modern civilization as stemming from the fact that human intelligence has tilted too much toward practicality, lacking in religious and spiritual aspects. With the rapid tempo of civilization, it is too overwhelming for individuals to digest and absorb within themselves, and it is also too difficult to distinguish between the fundamental currents and boundaries of civilization that become the ultimate goals of human life. 
Both spiritual civilization and material civilization are necessary for humanity, and there can be no good or evil in the speed or variety of civilization itself. However, humans must become the conscious subjects of civilization, regulating and balancing the whole. In this regard, I would like to express my beliefs on a more fundamental level as a substitute for my opening remarks. 
In a modern society where ideals and value systems have collapsed, establishing a fundamental value system is more urgently needed than anything else. However, humans living in a relative world cannot establish absolute values by themselves, nor can they possess the ability to pursue those values to the end. And absolute values cannot be discovered in any place or situation solely through the world of results. 
The realization of absolute values is also needed by the absolute being itself. Absolute values can only be found within the ideals (purposes) of the universe's first cause, and in conclusion, they can be found within the ideals of the absolute being, that is, within love. 
Absolute values are realized when harmonized and unified before the ideal of absolute love
All things have a dual purpose: a purpose that benefits the individual and a higher purpose that seeks harmony within the whole. Therefore, the universe is like a large organism composed of a dual-purpose continuum, and beings that achieve their individual purposes by completely uniting subject and object within themselves do not exist in isolation or a fixed state. 
Individuals take a subjective or objective position to relate to other beings, and by becoming one with them, they develop into beings with higher directional and purposive qualities. Thus, the universe is a common purpose entity connected by the common interests of subjects and objects, possessing some force or cosmic power that serves the common purpose of the entire universe. 
What is the content of the most profound and complete correlation for the eternal harmony and unity of subjects and objects? It is a relationship centered on love. The motivation for love does not start from humans. The ultimate source of love is the absolute, unchanging causal subject. As you know, in religion, this first cause is referred to as God. Throughout my life, I have had deep communion with God and have testified to His will and love through numerous experiences. 
What is the most important and necessary thing for God? God does not need knowledge. The wondrous harmony of this universe, which is the expression of omniscience, is evidence of that. He does not need money, power, or fame. The only thing that is absolutely necessary for God, who is the essence of love, is an object that can receive that love, that is, a being that He can love, and this object is manifested in the world of results. 
However, since humans, who are the central and total entity of the world of results, are the most precious object beings before the ideal of absolute love, the absolute being also desires the complete realization of His love ideal, that is, the realization of absolute values through humans. Therefore, the point at which the ideal of absolute love is realized centered on humans is the moment when humans are perfected as the object of the absolute being. In other words, when they harmonize and unite as relative objects before the love of the absolute subject, it becomes the point where the love ideal is realized. 
The resonance of love with the absolute being is the minimum standard for accessing the absolute realm
Then, what is the realm of human perfection, that is, what does it mean to be perfected as the object of the absolute being? The condition that the object must fulfill before the subject of love and perfect harmony is that the subject and object within itself must be completely harmonized and unified. Therefore, when humans achieve complete oneness of heart and body through personal growth centered on the absolute being, they will realize absolute love, and at that time, humans will enter the resonance of love with the absolute being. That is, when the heart and body are completely harmonized without any conflict, the resonance of love arises, and just as a tuning fork resonates, the resonance with the absolute being occurs automatically, which becomes the minimum standard for accessing the absolute realm in the relative world. 
The degree to which a person's mind and body are unified, how high and pure that degree is, determines the extent to which the subjective absolute world resonates and harmonizes with them. From this perspective, the human fall that religion speaks of refers to the state of humans having fallen before fully reaching the resonance of love with the absolute being, and salvation refers to the historical providence of restoring broken humans, like a tuning fork that cannot resonate, back to being resonant beings of love. 
When the mind and body become completely harmonized under absolute love, that is, when they become ideal individuals, they do not remain as individuals but take a subjective or objective position in relation to other individuals, establishing a developmental relationship of mutuality. The development of the love ideal must progress step by step according to the process of realizing the ideal of the absolute being, reaching higher dimensions. Therefore, the ideal individual, whose heart and body are completely united under absolute love, will develop into an ideal family together with another ideal individual, and this ideal family will develop into an ideal society, nation, and world, where the joy and happiness gained from the resonance of absolute love will spread and harmonize with the whole and eternity. 
The existing value system lacking the three-dimensional content of love must be reevaluated
Originally, love itself cannot be a means; it is a purpose, so the directionality of love itself determines the flat relative relationships or the vertical order of subject and object. Everything seeks to unite in love. Even amidst the misunderstanding and persecution of the wicked generation, the saints who practiced the path of love showed the way by sacrificing and giving, neutralizing the antagonism of the world. 
Absolute values must be thought of not in terms of knowledge but in terms of love, intertwined with emotion. Only love itself is the purpose, the completion, and the highest value. True love brings joy to the giver and joy to the receiver as well. Originally, love sprouts and is felt within the individual through nature, not learned. 
The world of knowledge is developed through cognition, but the world of emotion cannot be developed. Therefore, absolute values exist not in the dimension of knowledge but in the dimension of absolute love. In this regard, the first cause cannot be found within our cognitive rights but can be said to be experienced and felt on an emotional level. 
Values lacking the three-dimensional content of love cannot be eternal and unchanging; they will eventually flow away. Various strands of ideologies and thoughts up to now have, on one hand, helped humanity, but on the other hand, they have often misled humanity's ideological system and failed to lead history in a progressive manner. In that sense, I believe reevaluation of the existing value system is unavoidable. Furthermore, it is lamentable that many achievements in academic research in various fields are being misused due to confusion and distortion of the value system. 
I believe that those who feel these issues seriously and realize them first have a mission to unite and ensure that all academic achievements are properly utilized for humanity. Scholars should no longer remain bystanders in correcting distorted values. And I believe that this work should not be limited to any specific field of expertise, and that scholars from each field can achieve results by cooperating with a sense of mission. 
Respected representatives!

4. The Problem of Life and Eternal Life
How long do you think you will live? How long? Everyone thinks, "I will live until seventy or eighty." "Yes." Before that, do you not think about dying? "Yes." (Laughter) You are greedy, greedy. Even if I absolutely believe that I will die at eighty or a hundred, I do not know if I will die tomorrow or today. Do you know if you will die while eating? You have all those greedy thoughts, right? Do you have a guarantee from God? You should think that you might die as soon as possible, within a year. You must prepare everything in this short period. Live with that mindset. The shorter you think it is, the happier you will be. The shorter you think it is, the less loss you will have. The content of preparing sincerely during that short period is building your eternal house of life.

Then, in that short period, have you loved God? You want to become one with God and love God, but you cannot. God says, "Love." While living in the human world, introduce at least one person to God... Pour out all your sincerity 24 hours a day. If you live like that and die, that will be the subject of eternal life. Do you understand what I mean?

Crossroads of Life and Death 

Everything in our human life cannot escape the relationships of darkness and light, high and low, left and right, front and back. 

The issue of human life and death is determined by the smallest details. 

So, how about you now? Some of you may be feeling sleepy, while others are fully awake. (Laughter) Your hearts are the same. You may be sitting here now, but you want to go this way, you want to stay here, you want to go left, you want to go right—there are various positions. We know that. Some people like this place, and some dislike it. For some, coming this morning may be a blessing, while for others, it may be a misfortune. 

That’s why when we ask who should decide, it’s not the person next to you, nor the people in front or behind you; you must decide for yourself. You need to understand that. From this perspective, you must think seriously about how much you consider your life choices—whether to advance or retreat, or to go left or right. 

The rise and fall of humanity, success and failure, or life and death do not start from the big things. They start from the very small things. You hear something, and someone says something like, "That sounds plausible," or "That won’t work." You need to realize that misjudging these small things can determine the course of your entire life. By hearing something small and acting wrongly, life and death can be at stake.
You need to understand that this conflicting and tremendous result is connected. Now, if you take a step after hearing that and then turn back, it means that life and death are at stake here. It starts from that one step.

The same goes for what you see. Just feeling, “I wish I could be like that,” when you see something, itself influences such results. The same applies to words. If you hadn’t said that one word, such misfortunes wouldn’t have occurred, but by saying the wrong word, a tremendous issue in your life is determined. Next, our actions are the same. Even if you act without thinking, that action itself can lead to such tremendous results, which we can see often in our daily lives.

Where should the Unification Church go in such a situation?
So, in this situation, where should we go? We need to go to a higher place, a better place. That is a common notion among ordinary people. Then, what is a good and high place? A good place is one that everyone welcomes, and a bad place is one that everyone denies. A high place is where everyone desires to be. When you are in that position, everyone respects and seeks that position. This is something we know as human nature. So, is it easy for us to reach a good and high place in our daily lives? “It’s difficult.”

However, whether it’s you, people from the past who have come and gone, people living in the world now, or everyone who will come in the future, don’t you think everyone wishes for that? Looking at it this way, among all the people in the past who thought about going to a high place, would there be more successful people or more failures? “There would be more failures.” What about humanity worldwide right now? Will there be more successful people or more failures? “There are more failures.” What about the future world? The same principle operates through the past, present, and future, and that is a stark reality. You need to understand that it is a stark reality.

So, before solving this problem, which is like an equation, no matter how high and good a place you pursue, you will reach the conclusion that it is nothing more than an impossible dream. Then, looking at it centered around the members of the Unification Church, you should know that the high and good place the Unification Church desires is at a higher dimension than what ordinary people desire. Can we reach that place by following the path that those who have succeeded in human history have taken?

You are in the middle, and you are moving forward like this. The Unification Church is like this. Among them, there are those who go straight and those who go around. (Laughter) They are engaging in all sorts of activities like this. (Laughter) Where are you all going right now? Are you going straight, or are you going around? You know that well. “We are going straight.” Sometimes, people stab each other in the heart and kill each other. There are many such activities right now. Heaven and Hell
So, then, what is heaven and what is hell? Heaven is where God resides, and hell is where Satan resides. Heaven is a place that loves God, and hell is a place that mourns centered around Satan. Who is the king of heaven? It is God, and what does God like? Does God like rich people, powerful people, or wise people just because they came to heaven? Those kinds of people are all failures! It must be a place where God can rejoice with people who can love.

What kind of place is hell? Hell is a place that boasts of power, boasts of money, and boasts of oneself. Our true heart desires to receive love and demands goodness, but the opposite nature collides in all directions in hell. However, just because you are in hell does not mean the desire to receive love disappears. It becomes stronger, even more. How much… (The recording cuts off briefly)

Heaven is a place that wants to receive love, and even when it receives, it wants to receive more. What you all think is “good,” that one word “good” enters into a thousand words of “good.” When sleepy eyes come into contact with that love, they don’t know where sleep has run away to, and when ears that couldn’t hear come into contact with the heart of love, nothing is uncommunicable, and no scent is uncommunicable. It is a world of love where everything can whisper for 24 hours, for thousands of years. Our cells and all senses can move more than 100%. How much would you want that, how much? Think about how much you would want that. (Laughter and applause)

That’s why God also likes that love; does He like ordinary neighborly love or the love of today’s hippie groups? Is that good? “No.” Therefore, you should all look around. To go to a high place, one must stand in a low place in the Unification Church.

The Birth of Jesus and the Completion of God’s Will
Merry Christmas and Happy New Year! (Applause) Please sit down.
Today, we know that the whole world is celebrating the day of Jesus' birth. Originally, it is December 25th, but we have moved it forward to December 24th to celebrate today. Originally, our Unification Church decided to celebrate Christmas on January 3rd, but we have moved it forward to today to have this celebration. The title of the message I want to give you today is ‘The Birth of Jesus and the Completion of God’s Will.’ I will speak briefly on this title.
The completion of God’s will is centered on love and achieving the ideal of the son-in-law
We know that Jesus came to this earth not by his own will. He was born on this earth according to God’s will. And when Jesus was born, he did not come alone to fulfill God’s will. Ultimately, Jesus was born on the foundation that was prepared for 4,000 years, a nation that was organized to be able to unite with Jesus’ will at the same time as his birth. The nation of Israel was born to represent God’s will, and we must recognize that it has the absolute responsibility to inherit and complete the will of Jesus. Therefore, you should know that if God, the Messiah Jesus, and the nation of Israel do not unite centered on the will, all of God’s providential will cannot be completed.
Now, was Jesus originally a necessary being for us on this earth? We understand through the Principle that Jesus came to re-present God’s will because humanity fell. If humanity had not fallen, God’s will would have been completed, but ultimately, it was not completed due to the fall. God’s will had to be fulfilled through God, Adam and Eve, and all of Adam’s historical descendants, but because the foundation that had to be fulfilled through them was completely broken, Jesus had to come to re-present it, and the nation of Israel had to be re-organized.
The will of God is fulfilled by completing the ideal of creation. So what is God’s ideal of creation? Of course, creating all things is part of God’s ideal of creation, but it was to fulfill the ideal of creation centered on Adam and Eve. The completion of God’s ideal of creation, the completion of the will, is achieved by centering on God and God’s love, completing the ideal of the son-in-law, thus fulfilling both the ideal of creation and the will. You must understand this. In other words, the completion of God’s will always implies the foundation of love centered on God’s love and the love of the ideal son-in-law.
Therefore, there can be no completion of God’s will or realization of God’s ideal where God’s love departs. Originally, if humanity had not fallen, the love relationship between God and individual Adam would have been completed. Then, God and Eve would unite centered on love. Adam and Eve would unite centered on God’s love. And then all people would unite centered on God’s love with the united Adam and Eve.
Therefore, what is the center of everything? It is love. The unity of God and Adam and Eve is through love. The completion of the will is through love, and the realization of the ideal is completed through love; we must have this concept. Centered on that love, God and Adam and Eve become one, and then centered on that love, they become one with their children.
In our Unification Church, we call this relationship the completion of the three-object purpose centered on love. When viewed centered on Adam, it becomes God, Eve, and children; when viewed centered on the son, it becomes God, father, and mother; and when viewed centered on Eve, it becomes God, Adam, and children. This is what the three-object purpose means. You must establish the concept that I am representing within the realm of love centered on these three things, otherwise, you cannot maintain the realm of God’s love. This is the principled, original formula of the ideal of creation that must be united centered on God’s love.
Human beings have become self-centered beings due to the fall
Now, when we apply this principle to humanity in today’s world, everyone is in the position of parents and children centered on God. So what kind of world are we living in today? We are in the position of children centered on parents who are unrelated to God’s love. Because of the fall, the center of this world is not God but Satan. The grievance of becoming a child of Satan! You were not born with a blood relationship with God, but as children of Satan, you were born with a blood relationship with Satan. This enormous error is what the fall is, and it is a scary and fearful fact that we have not realized. What we are living in now is not centered on God’s love, but we are dealing with everything centered on self-centered love.
So what happened as a result of the fall? It is that I must love God, my mother, and my father centered on myself. It is to love centered on oneself.
Then, what is the original world that has not fallen like that? It is that I exist for the love centered on God, and I exist for the love centered on parents. You must understand this clearly. Until now, you have always thought you are in a subjective position, but you must understand that you should be in a relative position centered on God’s ideal, but due to the fall, you do not know that and everyone thinks they are the subject. Today’s fallen world is a world where this principle is completely inverted, leading to individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world being divided.
To correct this, God established religions, centered on Jacob, and created the foundation of victory over Satan to establish the chosen people’s rights. Then what is the nation of Israel, this chosen nation? It is a nation that has fought and won against Satan. You must understand that this victorious nation is fundamentally different from the realm of Satan.

When you consider the issue of Cain and Abel or such issues… Originally, to receive God’s blessing, one must be the firstborn. The second-born is not entitled to inherit God’s will. The fall...

Now go out and fight proudly

We must become Sunnies from Moonies. Do you understand? Therefore, when we advertise this time, we can say, 'Moonies will not end as Moonies but will become Sunnies. Home Church and the Completion of Heaven
<Prayer> Beloved Heavenly Father, we have just finished the year 1978. Now, the new year of 1979 has arrived for the Unification Church members around the world and all humanity. Reflecting once again on the hard work of our Father who has woven the path of suffering since the Fall, we recall the countless ancestors who failed to fulfill their responsibilities and trampled upon the providential heart, extending the ties of history to this day, continuing the sorrowful history.

Your deep heart has longed for the victory of a day, and we are reminded once again of the countless humans who have flowed silently into the unknown world through the history of tears and bloodshed. Among countless humans and nations, you chose the poor Korea and awakened this insignificant child among the chosen nation, training us from our foolish days until the day we recognized the time, allowing us to endure through countless persecutions and ultimately to occupy the glorious position of today. I feel this on January 1, 1979, at midnight, at the Belvedere training center.

Home Church and the Completion of Heaven
<Prayer> Beloved Heavenly Father, we have just finished the year 1978. Now, the new year of 1979 has arrived for the Unification Church members around the world and all humanity. Reflecting once again on the hard work of our Father who has woven the path of suffering since the Fall, we recall the countless ancestors who failed to fulfill their responsibilities and trampled upon the providential heart, extending the ties of history to this day, continuing the sorrowful history.

Your deep heart has longed for the victory of a day, and we are reminded once again of the countless humans who have flowed silently into the unknown world through the history of tears and bloodshed. Among countless humans and nations, you chose the poor Korea and awakened this insignificant child among the chosen nation, training us from our foolish days until the day we recognized the time, allowing us to endure through countless persecutions and ultimately to occupy the glorious position of today. This is all your grace, and we once again praise your holy work.

Father, the countless ancestors in the spirit world and all the prophets and saints who have come and gone bearing the historical sorrow are looking upon this place at this time, waiting for a new historical proclamation. I feel this on January 1, 1979, at midnight, at the Belvedere training center.

This is not a dream; it is reality. This means the rabbit is jumping to escape. (laughter) So you all will start jumping from tomorrow. Then you will receive God's blessings.

Starting from the New Year, the teacher will not be here. I will be wandering around. I will be wandering through England. You all will think, even if I am not here, that I am here, right? "Yes." Moreover, the leaders…. Are all the main leaders gathered? From now on, you all should plan to live for about three years without taking off your clothes or loosening your ties. When you return to your headquarters, clear out all the beds. Clear out the beds and rooms of the leaders, everything. If possible, sleep and pray in the guest room or living room. So that it is cold and hard, and you will think, 'Oh, I hope the day breaks soon. It would be nice to go out.' That's what I want you to do. Do you understand what I'm saying? "Yes." This is what the leaders should do. So, I will not allow the leaders to stay in the New Yorker building either.

Leaders here, since the teacher has said this, do it voluntarily. If you don't, I will make Kamiyama do it. The teacher is still sitting in a chair like this and sleeping a lot. After sending you all away, I often sit up here and sleep like this. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Until now, your way of thinking that 'this will work' will not do. If your juniors inherit that tradition, it will be a big problem, a big problem.

From now on, all businesses are side businesses. What is the main business? It is evangelism, evangelism. The time spent evangelizing should exceed the time spent working. Otherwise, can you save the 240 million people in America? Even if it means sacrificing all of you, God's thought is to save America. Therefore, He wants you to sacrifice and endure hardships.

Look. The time is now just like the time when you offered your one and only beloved Jesus on the cross. It is the same. This is not for Reverend Moon, nor for the Unification Church, but for America, the world, and God. For justice…. Is that not a principled statement? "It is a principled statement." Then you must do it, you must.

Now go out and fight proudly
So, since we made a promise, believe it…. Then tomorrow, you will welcome the New Year in God's blessings, and as proud individuals, from now on, if anyone insults you and calls you a Moonie, you must hold them and engage in theoretical struggle. We must become Sunnies from Moonies. Do you understand? If all the American people forget that we are Moonies and can call us Sunnies, then it will be the time when our intentions can spread globally. Therefore, when we advertise this time, we can say, 'Moonies will not end as Moonies but will become Sunnies. From now on, our Unification Church will not remain silent to those who call us Moonies, but will remain silent to those who call us Sunnies.' Just add that one line. (laughter) We must hold onto those who call us Moonies and discuss it theoretically. Ask them why they call us Moonies…. To my friends in America
Dear friends!
You may have heard stories about me over the past few years. Whether those stories have been good or bad, I would like you to forget them all and for the next five minutes, I would like to ask you a few questions.
Please read this letter to understand those questions.
The reason I am writing this letter to you is that I have an important message that I must share with you. And I believe this message is a matter of life for you.
Recently, I received a very heartwarming letter from a young American living in New York named Mark Barry. In that letter, he said the following:
"Since I learned about the revelations that you received from God, my entire life has completely changed. Not only did I come to know what kind of being God is, but I also came to understand what kind of being I am. At the same time, I have been able to sincerely love others, something I could never have practiced in the past. This is my heartfelt gratitude to you, Teacher Moon."
Meanwhile, a letter was sent by a mother of one of our Unification Church members, Pegev Moffitt, who lives in Midland, Texas, with the following content:
"I am now kneeling down and thanking you and God. I earnestly pray that God will bless Teacher Moon, who has raised countless young people before Him, with the gospel. Teacher Moon has done what I could never do for my children."
Dear friends! I once again thank God.
The reason is that there are tens of thousands of people on this planet who are grateful just like that one mother. Since they learned the content of the revelations I received from God, amazing things have happened to them. Numerous miracles are occurring. Young people are overcoming drug problems. They are escaping from mental illnesses. And countless physical ailments are being healed. Moreover, they have gained a fresh hope and have come to know what the purpose of life is. They are discovering a new familial way to become one in God's love.
At the same time, they have been able to overcome the barriers that divide nations and have come to understand that all people are true brothers and sisters in God's one family, transcending nationalism. They have learned how to live as true brothers and sisters.
Dear friends! Just like those people, you too can live joyfully and happily. This is the reason I am writing this letter to you. I am not revealing the many amazing things I have accomplished so far. I firmly believe that with God's power, nothing is impossible.
What we need most importantly is to gain a new understanding of God. We need to know the new truth, and we need to know God's new revelations. This new revelation from God is now being revealed to you. This revelation can become yours.
Today, there is not a single person who does not have difficult problems. Every individual, every family, every nation, and this world is now struggling in despair to solve their respective problems. However, it seems that there are no practical solutions. Countless cries of lament are heard in despair. Just last year, the number of Americans who committed suicide reached 38,000.
People are trying in various ways to solve their individual problems. But only God can solve them.
God has a clear plan for this humanity. And He has a plan for how we should live our lives.
And I believe that the revelations I received provide the best content for understanding that God. The importance of you knowing this new truth lies here.
Dear friends! My experience of coming to know God began when I was 16 years old.
From my youth, I began to ponder various fundamental questions about life. 'Who am I? Where did I come from? What is the purpose of life? Does our life continue after death? And does God really exist? Is God omnipotent or powerless? If God is omnipotent, why does He not solve the problems of humanity? Why is there so much suffering on this earth?'
In any case, for the next nine years, I lived with the omnipotent God and Jesus. I entered the spirit world several times. Gradually, God taught me astonishing truths. It was like a long, dark night passing and the morning sun rising. In that truth, I was able to see the dawn of a glorious new culture.
This special revelation based on the New Testament is far superior to the teachings of Judaism. This revelation has the power and ability to encompass all religions and unite them. The revelation I received is now called 'The Principle,' and I have been instructed by God to spread this principle to the ends of the earth.
When I first began teaching this truth under the North Korean regime, I was persecuted by both Christianity and the communist regime. I was imprisoned by communists and served about three years in a forced labor camp. It was a place designed to gradually kill people. In that situation, I was able to survive only by God's power.
One day before I was to be executed, I was rescued by the UN forces involved in the Korean War. So, I was able to come down to the free world of South Korea.
In 1954, I officially founded the Unification Church in Seoul, Korea. Four years later, I sent missionaries to Japan. In a short span of 25 years, our movement spread to 127 countries across six continents. And now, the Principle is being taught in every language of the world.
In 1971, God gave me another revelation, telling me to go quickly to America, where millions were waiting for the new revelation from God. God instructed me to spread the message in America because this country was chosen to play a bridging role in connecting humanity worldwide.
In just seven years, I traveled through all 50 states of America, spreading the content of the new revelation. As a result, I was able to connect with millions of Americans, and now the Unification Church is being established from Maine to Hawaii. During my travels in America, I was deeply impressed many times by the greatness of the American spirit and its material achievements.
However, now I see this great nation surrounded by worrying problems. Millions of families are being destroyed. Young people are experiencing relentless turmoil.
Crime and violence are rampant. Therefore, my heart feels severe pain. In the name of God, who loves America, I have made countless pledges to do my utmost to help this country. I am confident that the revelation I received will instill a new image in America and elevate this country to a new nobility and greatness.
Some people who criticize what I do say that I brainwash the American people. I find that expression interesting. When I spoke before members of Congress in 1975, I said, 'I have one question for you. Can you be so foolish and dumb as to be brainwashed by this Korean person? I cannot think that way at all.' After I finished speaking, a congressman came to me, shook my hand, and said, 'Teacher Moon, I really did not expect you to give such a perfect answer.' And recently, in 1978, the U.S. Department of Justice concluded that the members of the Unification Church..."
"It is legal, and I believe we are adults who can agree." I have expressed that the things I have accomplished so far have not been achieved by my own strength, but by the power of God. The real feeling of joy and vitality that people experience is given as a result of experiencing God's spirit.

Dear friends! If you come into contact with God's truth and become ignited, you will no longer be able to live an ordinary life. The world will become your stage. You will become involved in helping others and fighting against injustice. When you receive God's inspiration, you will condemn war. However, you will be responsible for a different kind of struggle, which is to accomplish the work for humanity to eliminate poverty, disease, and ignorance.

Members of the Unification Church know deeply that all people are precious sons and daughters of God. They transcend the color of skin and treat each other as true brothers and sisters. They are realizing a world where God's families live within "living colors." The work of building a world family in God is an exciting adventure. 

This is the reason why there can be no monotonous or boring moments for the members of our Unification Church. This is something you can understand if you ask them. Their every day is filled with excitement and accomplishment. They are practitioners, not just believers in the truth.

Dear friends! Now you will discover the value of the principle without feeling any sense of duty. I do not ask you to become members of our Unification Church or to support our church. I only wish to give you the opportunity to understand this significant and vital message.

As detailed in the pamphlet printed in color enclosed with this letter, there are three special programs prepared for your participation:

1. You can attend the "Feast of Hope."
This program is a two-hour event featuring songs, dances, music, and the introduction of God's new revelations. It takes place every Tuesday at 7 PM at the World Mission Center located at 481 Eighth Avenue, Manhattan, and admission is free. You can enjoy this time with your family. (You can request tickets as needed using the response form enclosed with this letter.)

2. You can attend a one-day seminar on the principle.
This one-day seminar is a program that outlines the principles in a short time, starting every Saturday at 10 AM at the World Mission Center. Here, you will have the opportunity to understand astonishing new truths in just one day. Through this program, you will have a joyful experience. (To register for the seminar, please use the enclosed response form.)

3. You can schedule a home lecture course on the principle.
When it is difficult for you to leave your home, you can sit at home and listen to lectures covering the entire content of the principle through this home lecture course. This lecture will open a new dimension in your life. (To attend this lecture, please use the enclosed response form. You can find more details in the pamphlet.)

Through any of these programs, you will receive the greatest gift I can offer. This gift will be more wonderful than any you have received on any past birthday or Christmas because it is given by God.

Of course, you may be indifferent to this unique opportunity. However, if you miss this chance, which occurs once in a million, you will come to regret it.

I look forward to your response. Please take a look at the enclosed response form to send your reply. I would appreciate it if you could use the prepaid envelope to send your response to me today. Then, I will promptly send you a reply. In the meantime, I sincerely wish for God's blessings to be upon you, your family, and your endeavors.

If you would like to have your name added to my prayer list, please write down your name and send it to me. Please refer to P.O. Box 4 to send your response form. The power of prayer brings about miracles. I would consider it a great honor to be able to pray for you and your loved ones.

Restored Families
You may have felt that the exchange between the Eastern and Western worlds is extremely difficult. For this exchange to happen, there must be a common language and writing. Otherwise, it cannot happen. Therefore, for those who are uninterested, it is like news from a distant country.

Western civilization has gone through a history to meet Eastern civilization, and if we view the East and West from God's perspective, it is like twins. In terms of purpose, the East originally advanced culturally ahead of the West. Ancient civilizations developed around the East. Greek civilization and Hebrew civilization are civilizations within the Eastern sphere. Hellenism and Hebraism started and intertwined within the Eastern sphere.

Thus, today, Western civilization is going through a history to meet Eastern civilization. Originally, it should have started in the East and gone to the West, but it is now returning from the West. If Jesus had not died, it would have been centered around Jesus and developed in the East, but now it is going to Rome and returning in reverse.

On January 21, 1979, at the Belvedere Training Center.
* This message is also published in the third issue of <True Family>, which is published in Japan.

Originally, Christianity should have been based on Confucianism and Buddhism. If Christianity had been connected and combined with Greek civilization and Egyptian civilization, the world's civilizations would have all merged. However, it went to Rome and became entangled there. Thus, the time has come for the world to revolve around the United States, connecting with Asia.

This is where the problems arise. There are issues between Asia and Western society. Conflicts keep arising. While it may seem bad that problems arise, it is there that unity occurs. What is destined to break will break, and what is meant to unite will unite.

Currently, the only country in the Western world that can connect with Asia is South Korea. It is holding onto the southern tip of Korea. There is only South Korea.
