What can erase this? “True love.”  
Can God Himself do that? Is there true love in the human world? “No.” Then what should be done? ‘Oh, I love God, so please come.’ Would He say, ‘Okay, I’m coming’? He wouldn’t believe it. He wouldn’t believe it. So, in the way of opposition, even if God kicks and hits and says, ‘What is this child?’ He must think, ‘I deserve to die a hundred times, a thousand times.’  
What about God? If Adam and Eve had not fallen and had loved, they would have been in love, and if they were kicked out, they could oppose. That’s why people in the fallen world cannot love unless they are at least at the level of a person who can oppose. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.”  
So, a person who lives to receive God’s love, that is, a person who lives to love God can say to God, ‘Please come.’ God can claim, ‘The person who is in a position above the restored Adam is like this because of this.’ The conclusion is that there cannot be anything other than that miserable position I just mentioned. Because such a person has not appeared until now, it concludes that there has been no one whom God could love in history. In the era of the Unification Church, it is the first time to say, let’s do this centered on Reverend Moon. (Applause)  
When Reverend Moon steps forward for His will, ‘God, I know this. So, mobilize the people of the world to attack Reverend Moon. Mobilize all the satanic forces in the universe to attack. In the end, let God attack. Still, I will go. Isn’t that the only way to heal Your wounded heart of love?’ Then God answers, ‘That’s right.’ That’s why Reverend Moon faces opposition. Is that bad or good? “It’s good.” You must understand that it becomes a fundamental ideology that can draw down God’s pure love onto the Earth.  
So, what about you? If the people of the world oppose the Unification Church and Reverend Moon, what will you do? ‘Oh, what is this… What is the Unification Church, what is this Moon Sun Myung? What happened to God?’ Will you say that? “No.” This is a statement that fits the theory. It is a statement that fits the theory.  
You had your first love, but if the other person defiled it, to heal the defilement, that person must enter a position where they die for you hundreds of times. So, if they sacrifice for you, and do it over and over, then naturally, their heart will emerge, and they can forgive and let go. It’s the same. God is the same as us.  
Because there has been no such person, until now, God’s love has not been able to come down to this Earth. If such a person exists on Earth, would God come to see them? “He will come.” Even if you put up flyers saying, ‘God, don’t come,’ and do everything to oppose Him, God will follow you. He follows you from the unseen. (Laughter) That’s why when Reverend Moon is in a place of death or solitude, He says, ‘Hey, hey, I am here.’ Do you understand what that means? “Yes.” Otherwise, He cannot fulfill His will.  
You must suffer more to liberate God and humanity.
man, beautiful woman, I will not seek after them. I will seek after the one who is the worst, and I will become the best wife or husband.’ That is the principle you should establish. 

You should think, ‘Even if I meet the worst husband or wife, I will become the best spouse.’ This is the attitude you need to have. 

Now, if you want to be a great person, you need to go through hardships. You need to go through trials and tribulations. If you want to be a great wife or husband, you need to endure and overcome difficulties. 

This is how you can achieve greatness. You need to be willing to face opposition and challenges. 

In this way, you will be able to create a restored family. A restored family is one that loves all people, transcends all nations, and loves beyond all classes. Only then can you overcome. 

You need to understand that in a restored family, God is present. Therefore, you must love God. You must return to your first love. 

This restored family, as I mentioned earlier, must go through trials. It is not enough for a white person to suffer among white people. A white person must go to Africa and suffer there. Conversely, black people must come to the white world and suffer. Only then can the world become one. 

If we do not do this, there is no way to unite. 

The God who is the most pitiful in the world is our Lord, the Lord of families, the Lord of nations, the Lord of the world, and the Lord of the universe. We must understand that there is no way to unite except through the path of oneness. 

Who does this benefit? It benefits my family, my nation, my world, and my universe. One person represents all of this. 

The reason you cannot complain about Reverend Moon is that you realize, ‘Oh, the teacher has suffered more than us, and he has endured global hardships for us.’ That is the only reason. 

Even while suffering outside, you think, ‘I must suffer more.’ Is that true? 

This path, the path to restore God's first love, cannot be walked by anyone other than those who are struggling. There is no other way to make the world one. 

Therefore, we, the Unification Church members, must absolutely align with this ideology. We must align with this ideology. 

When you apply this love to people, it becomes yeast and cannot help but turn into wine. There is no one who cannot become one, whether man or woman. All fighting and lies will be driven away. When you apply that love, it becomes yeast and dissolves everything. 

Unification Church members must know who they should follow. Even if five people live in one room, if they do not work, try to make others serve them, sleep early, and do not offer anything, they cannot be the owner. 

The one who suffers more than others and is silent is the true owner. If your eyes are sparkling just for yourself, and if everything is going well for you, you cannot be the owner. 

Unification Church members are the opposite. It is the opposite of the world. The world operates one way, but heaven operates the opposite way. 

Here, our Unification Church women may wear a lot of makeup, but during the time spent on makeup, God would prefer if you cleaned the offerings and did the laundry for the whole community. 

Those who do that will go to a different place. Those who are self-serving will go elsewhere. Even if they have entered the Unification Church, they will leave. 

In the world, the only person who has succeeded while being criticized is Reverend Moon. This will be recorded throughout history. 

Even President Nixon of the United States fled after a year and a half of trouble, but Reverend Moon does not run away even when beaten. 

Now those people say, ‘We have lost.’ They say it themselves. The New York Times and the Washington Post say, ‘We have lost,’ and even the U.S. Congress says, ‘We have lost.’ 

Do Unification Church members say that? No. You know it, don’t you? Who made that happen? Was it Reverend Moon? No. Was it America? No. It was God who did that. 

Now, do you understand how great our God is? 

We must establish a tradition of love that serves and elevates in the restored family. 

The earth rotates once a day, and it has undoubtedly been spinning for millions of years. It must be spinning like that. 

If the time changes by even one second, what would happen? This large earth spins without a second of error. It goes for billions of years without a second of error. 

When you see this, you realize how meticulous God is. 

When you reach such a position, that God is always with you. Whether it is a thousand years or ten thousand years, He will be with you. 

Do you know such a God? We believe in such a God in the Unification Church. We love such a God more than anyone else. We fight with such a God. 

My loving heart must remain unwavering for a thousand years or ten thousand years, just as the earth spins for tens of thousands of years without error. My heart must not differ by even a second or a penny. 

That is how you must love God. Are you doing that? 

Do you want to go up and down in love, or do you want to do it forever? What is it? 

Then you can have God in your restored family, and you can be the husband of a restored family, the wife of a restored family, and the children of a restored family. 

Is that a difficult thing or an easy thing? 

It is a difficult thing. That is why, unmarried young women and men, you must dream, ‘Even if I meet the ugliest man or woman, I will go this way.’ You must establish this principle. 

‘I will not seek after good looks; I will seek after the one who is the worst, and I will become the best spouse.’ That is the principle you should establish.
"I have to meet my husband and then my wife." If you decide like this, everything falls apart. That's how you think. What does God do? God carries out this kind of operation. He puts masks on everyone's face, covering them with the mask of the ugliest person, and sends them to the wedding ceremony. Then, at the wedding ceremony, He removes the masks. It could happen like that. But don't think like that. You shouldn't think that way and act accordingly. Those who go with the mindset of meeting the ugliest person should understand that God blesses them even more.

So, do you love God? "Yes." Do you really love God? "Yes." When God appears and says, "I am God," He is born as a crippled baby, defecates in His place, and then grows up to be a young man who marries a woman just as crippled as He is, and they have many children who are all like them. Would you be able to love them as they die one by one? And this God, He says, "You little brats! Why is dinner late? It's time to sleep, why are you bringing it late? Why are you making me wait when I need to pee?" and even hits them. (Laughter) So, would you still love Him? "Yes." Would you still love Him, even so? "Yes." Loving a person like that is the same as how you treat God.

In American families, don't they all try to send their grandparents to nursing homes as quickly as possible? Can they go to heaven like that? "No." Then, is it the way to love God to take care of the grandparents living in nursing homes, cleaning their mess and serving them? "Yes." If there is a girl in the neighborhood doing such work, wouldn't the neighborhood say, "This girl is ruining our America and our nursing homes. Let's kill her." Would they protest? "No." Do you think anyone would protest? "No."

What will you choose? Do you members of the Unification Church want to send your grandparents to nursing homes or not? "We won't send them." What will you do when Reverend Moon comes to your house and says he will grow old and die there? Won't you say, "Oh no, no. There are Yejin and Hyojin, so please go to your children's house"? Wouldn't you say that? "No." If you are like that, are you better than me? (Laughter) I tried to do that too, but I couldn't because I didn't have the time. My parents have all passed away.

Families are in love... Love is something that burns in caring for one another, and you must understand that it ignites in uplifting each other and shines brightly. We must establish such traditions in this restored family.

Let's build a fortress of love in home church.
Now, American families are collapsing. They are collapsing. They have already all collapsed. The world has all collapsed. Everyone in the satanic world is collapsing. So, is this teaching needed in America or not? "It is needed." The young people who are just playing around need to work hard for the world, sweating for it, and even working 24 hours is not enough; they are in a position where there is so much work that they can't sleep. Is that a game for America to collapse or to prosper?

And then, going to God's position, this ideology... "Ah, amazing and grateful God!" For a thousand years, for ten thousand years, no matter what price I have to pay in my life, I must realize that standing before Him, standing in His love, is so insufficient. You must understand this amazing fact. Right now, you may be miserable, but in 10 years, in 20 years, you will become great. That is undoubtedly true, just by looking at me.

In the past, even if I waited 24 hours for someone to come, not a single person would visit, but now, even if I tell them not to come, they line up to visit. Do you understand? "Yes." If I ask anyone, they say Reverend Moon has succeeded globally. That is an undeniable conclusion. When the same God goes with the same heart, He receives the same guarantee. This is the principle of heaven and earth.

So, go back to your families. To return to your families, you must fight in two nations. You must cross paths in two nations, then in two ethnic groups, then among two brothers, and finally between two parents. (While pointing to the board) You must cross paths between the communist world and the democratic world, and the center among them is the free world. Even in the free world, Cain and Abel are divided. In the nation, they are divided, and in the church, they are divided. Even within the Unification Church itself, there are divisions. This wall always exists. (While pointing to what he wrote)

So now, you must find Cain-like home churches and Abel-like home churches centered around home church. You must also find your family back in your hometown. (While pointing to what he wrote)

So, you must walk that path. Don't think that there is no one who can love me; rather, think regretfully about what I have failed to love. God does not lament because there is no one to love Him, but He laments for not being able to love, so continue with that heart. God is the first to love. Therefore, when you enter the family centered on love, you must become a victor who can say that there are no misfortunes or blockages anywhere.

When you stand in this family and look out at the restored world, if you have walked a path so dreadful that you don't even want to think about it, the more dreadful that path has been, the happier you are. So, the struggles and hardships you have gone through are for meeting this wife and this husband, for meeting these sons and daughters. You stand in a position where you can't even think about restoration, not even in your dreams. Therefore, let our families be filled with songs of love. Let us love our wives like God loves and our sons and daughters like God loves.

We must think that our home has walked the path of suffering that can erase the traces of God's first love while establishing love. Here, no matter how much Satan tries to penetrate, nothing can penetrate. Nothing can destroy it. So, how do we build this wall? We build it through home church. That is why home church is precious. All these struggles have been compressed and concentrated into the essence of home church, which has been entrusted to you to take away from all the people in the world.

Why do I give that to you? Why? Wouldn't it be better without it? How nice would it be to just go in without that? If you don't do that, you can go in and out as much as you want. Do you understand? "Yes." So, it is about creating a wall in the era of entering the family of happiness. It is about building a fortress-like wall. That is like building a castle. So, how hard is that? The harder it is, the better it is. The harder it is, the better it is.

You must completely love and pass through home church for the universe to become yours.
So, at this time when all Unification Church members can establish such home churches, it is indeed a remarkable victory that transcends national borders, tribes, nations, religions, and all cultures. It is as if thousands of years of history are jumping forward. That is why even if I die now, I don't need the term "Second Coming" for restoration. Because you have completed all of this, it means that it is not needed. You can live in the infinite spiritual world that God has arranged, enjoying a banquet with God every day for millions of years.

In the future, when the teacher says, "I am going to any star," will you follow or not? "I will follow." If you go like this, you will meet. You will have a joyous banquet. There are no owners on all the stars of this universe right now. That is why I say to you, "You be the owners. It is okay for you to be the owners." You might think, "Oh, won't everything fall apart?" But since the spiritual world transcends time and space, you can see everything. You can see everything. No matter how far away it is, if you see it, you will know everything. (Applause) Look. That is not a dream; it is reality, not a dream but reality.

That is why a smart person like Reverend Moon, who can succeed elsewhere, is acting like this because he knows that. That is why he is playing this game. Why do you follow the teacher? Because your hearts already know and judge and follow. So, to act freely, you must go through the family. You must completely love in the restored family and go. If you pass there, the whole universe becomes yours. God also becomes yours.

Here, what kind of man or woman do you want to meet to go to heaven? "An ugly man." "An ugly woman." Do you understand that clearly? "Yes." Do you know how you should live and go? "Yes." The more you work until your hands are cut off and your feet are bent, the better it is. That is the same as the earth. The higher the degree of love, the higher you rise. The infinite universe can become your stage of activity. Do you understand? "Yes." The computer of the spiritual world is merciless. It records everything as it is.

Sometimes, you close your mouth, squint your eyes, and make your ears small to try to see God, to hear God's voice, and to want to talk to God. Staying up all night, you might say, "Tonight, I want to see God before I sleep, but I can't see Him," and you might cry. Then, at that moment, you will see. That is why it is precious.

Do you now have confidence that you can establish a restored family? "Yes." Are you confident? "Yes." What do you need to build the wall? "Love." It is love, but where do you love? "Home church." Home church is the world. It is a microcosm of the world. That is why all kinds of people are there. In America, all kinds of people live. There are black people, Spanish people, Korean people, Japanese people, all kinds of people, people of all colors live there.

Now, the interesting thing is that when you go to home church, even if you go, white people oppose it, saying "No." Instead, black people welcome you. Isn't that right? They oppose it. That is how it becomes. That is why white people prefer to visit the homes of black and colored people rather than white people. That is how we are restoring. So, you must understand how much history is leaping forward. You might find it hard to go around doing home church activities and dislike working, but you must understand that the historical environment is brightening day by day, heading towards the dawn, to meet the morning sunlight.

You must establish a restored family that receives God's love in home church.
So, what are you in home church? You are the Messiah, the Messiah. You must become the Messiah and achieve the opposing ideals there, giving birth to sons and daughters and seeking the restored family.

Then, do you want to live in a New Yorker building or go live in the home church neighborhood? "Home church." So, do you live in home church now? "Yes." What do you do there? You serve, serve. You must serve physically, serve mentally, and serve with love. It is a re-creation, a re-creation. You are re-creating. Depending on how much sweat and time you invest there, the standard for welcoming you changes. Also, depending on how much opposition you face... Even if you face opposition once, twice, or face opposition from everyone, if you stay calm, they will say, "There are no young people like that in America..." and immediately welcome you. All those boundaries will disappear and collapse. The walls that opposed Reverend Moon in America will start to crumble, right? "Yes." How wonderful is that story?

So, when you think like that, it becomes exciting. Without a doubt, it will collapse. When I fought with Congressman Fraser, I said, "No matter how strong it is, it will collapse. Fight." So, I fought. Mr. Park also didn't believe it at first. What the teacher has done until now is like that. It is all like that. "Oh, that sounds like a dream; can that really happen?" So, do you believe that the walls of the spiritual world have all collapsed and the walls of the world have all collapsed? Do you believe it?

Now, whether it is the Soviet Union, China, or North Korea, through the history of the spiritual world, our Unification Church side is emerging. Our side. The smartest sons and daughters, those capable of handling the theories of communism, are coming to the Unification Church... They say that what their fathers are doing is wrong. You may not know it, but such history is happening in the spiritual world right now.

Just like if a big dam bursts thousands of miles away, it takes days for the water to fill here. "Wow. Reverend Moon was right! Wow, Reverend Moon did that ten years ago." That is what they will say. So, you must be prepared to be able to be ready at any time. Don't think that the past and today are the same.

Twenty years ago in Korea, when I said that young Americans, Americans, and people from all over the world would come to find the teacher, everyone said it was a lie. (Laughter) You are the same. When I talk about what heaven is like, you all think the same. "No." You are a bit better than Koreans. "That's right." (Laughter)

So, you must think that you should now go live in home church. Pack your bags and keep going out from New Yorker.

Now, Mr. Young-Woon, please talk about your home church activities in England, starting from America, and tell us which people have developed and which people have been welcomed.

So, everyone, I ask you to become the undeniable owners of families, excellent owners, and create families that receive God's love. (Applause) *
